[29.11.2022, 15:47:16] ~â€¯Mohamed Ajmi: mon explication slack:
Hello everyone,
Some elements that can help you understand the difference in Q28.
This difference comes from how you standardize your DataFrame, more specifically if you re-arrange the columns (with ColumnTransformer).
I asked 
@Roberto Ceraolo
 about it and we concluded that using the column transformer is correct and it is better to re-arrange the columns to train the models as it was given in the original DataFrame.
